<p dir="auto"><i>  Building solutions with open source.</i><br><br></p>
<p dir="auto">ðŸ‘‹ Hi! I'm Anmol Baranwal, a full-stack developer from India, super into Open Source, and working as a Technical writer for international brands.</p>
<p dir="auto">ðŸ”¥ I have worked with more than 8 international teams like <a href="https://github.com/Avaiga/taipy">Taipy</a>, <a href="https://github.com/CopilotKit/CopilotKit">CopilotKit</a>, <a href="https://github.com/winglang/wing">Wing</a>, reaching an audience of over <em>200k</em>. If you need a technical writer, DM me on Twitter or LinkedIn.</p>
<p dir="auto">ðŸ”–   As a top author on <a href="https://dev.to/anmolbaranwal" rel="nofollow">dev.to/anmolbaranwal</a>, my content has been featured in prestigious communities like GitHub, resulting in a follower base of over <em>20k+</em> within 6 months.</p>
<p dir="auto">ðŸš€   I've established myself in the <a href="https://github.com/anuraghazra/github-readme-stats?tab=readme-ov-file#github-stats-card">Top 5%</a> of GitHub by contributing to <em>40+</em> projects with <em>200+</em> Pull Requests, participating in <em>500+</em> discussions, and earning a lot of reputation.</p>
<p dir="auto">ðŸŽ“   A 100% scholar in CS, I've played a crucial role as a maintainer &amp; contributor of <a href="https://github.com/rupali-codes/LinksHub">LinksHub</a> to turn it into an open source success story. <p dir="auto">ðŸ¤   I have learned a lot about the Open Source ecosystem during the past 2 years so I'm guiding others to start their journey with open source in multiple communities on Discord &amp; WhatsApp.</p>
<p dir="auto">ðŸŽ   I create helpful tips on open source, write about 2 open source projects daily, and a lot more to help you grow <code>"1% every day"</code> on <a href="https://twitter.com/Anmol_Codes" rel="nofollow">Twitter</a> and <a href="https://www.linkedin.com/in/Anmol-Baranwal/" rel="nofollow">LinkedIn</a>. <p dir="auto">I've been active across various platforms, whether it's for learning, creating content, trying the platform, or sharing my progress. I've tried a lot of stuff which is why I have a good knowledge of various domains.</p>
